function checkIsCanonicalHttps() {
    try {
        let linkTag = document.head.querySelector("link[rel='canonical']")
        if(linkTag) {
            let url = linkTag.href;
            if(url.startsWith("http://")) {
                linkTag.setAttribute("href", window.location.href)
                console.log("[SEO TRICKS] Found canonical link tag with http, changed to https!");
            } else {
                console.log("[SEO TRICKS] Canonical link tag is correct, exiting...");
            }
        } else {
            console.log("[SEO TRICKS] No canonical link tag found.");
        }
    } catch(error) {
        console.log(`[SEO TRICKS] Error setting the canonical tag with https`, error);
    }
}

                eventName: eventName,
                callback: callback
            })
            return `id_${window.TLH_LifeCycle.subscriberList.length}` 
        },
        unSubscribe: function (id) {}
    }
}

const urlsToRemoveAmpTag = [/^https?:\/\/www.lastampa.it\/esteri\/(.*\/)?video\//, /^https?:\/\/www.lastampa.it\/spettacoli\/(.*\/)?video\//, /^https?:\/\/www.lastampa.it\/la-zampa\/(.*\/)?video\//]


function kw_js_seo_tricks() {
  // resets itself avoiding further executions due to readystate change
  window.kw_js_seo_tricks = function() { };
  console.log("[SEO TRICKS] Adding seo meta");

  if(!window.pageType) {
    console.log("[SEO TRICKS] Missing pagetype....aborting");
    return;
  }
  setPageSEO();
  removeAmpTag(urlsToRemoveAmpTag)
  // modifyDOM();
}

function removeAmpTag(urls) {
  try {
    let ampLink = document.head.querySelector('link[rel="amphtml"]');
    console.log(`[SEO TRICKS] Attempt removal of amp tag`);

    for(let i = 0;i < urls.length;i++) {
      let url = urls[i];

      if(ampLink && url.test(window.location.href)) {
        ampLink.remove();
        console.log(`[SEO TRICKS] Amp link tag removed in ${url}!`);
        return
      }
    }
    console.log(`[SEO TRICKS] No amp tag was found or we're in the wrong page!`);
  } catch(e) {
    console.log(`[SEO TRICKS] Error eliminating the amp tag.`, e);
  }
}

function setPageSEO() {
  try {
    if(window.pageType === "lista_tag") {
      console.log("[SEO TRICKS] Looping SEO rules");
      let urls = config.modifySEOTitleAndDescription.urls;

      for(var i = 0;i < urls.length;i++) {
        if(window.location.href.indexOf(urls[i].url) > -1) {
          console.log("[SEO TRICKS] Matched current url with rule: ", urls[i].url, "- TITLE ", urls[i].title, " - DESCRIPTION ", urls[i].description);
          document.title = urls[i].title;
          document.querySelector("meta[name=description]").setAttribute("content", urls[i].description);
          console.log("[SEO TRICKS] Added seo meta");
          return;
        }
      }
      console.log("[SEO TRICKS] Didn't match any rule.");
    } else {
      console.log("[SEO TRICKS] Wrong pagetype.");
    }
  } catch(e) {
    console.log("[SEO TRICKS] ERROR EXECUTING SEO TRICKS", e);
  }
}

if(document.readyState !== 'loading') {
  window.kw_js_seo_tricks();
} else {
  document.onreadystatechange = function() {
    if(document.readyState !== 'loading') {
      window.kw_js_seo_tricks();
    }
  }
}

  (function () {
    var startDate = new Date("Apr 22, 2024 00:00").getTime() / 1000;
    var endDate = new Date("Apr 22, 2024 23:59:59").getTime() / 1000;
    var timer = function () {
      var now = new Date().getTime() / 1000;
      /* var now = kw_nowdate_epoch; 	 */
      if (now > startDate && now < endDate) {
        document.body.classList.add("has-special-logo");
      }
    }
    timer();
  })();
</script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        var as21DashboardScrollPos;
        var as21DashboardScrollContainer;
        var as21DashboardScrollArrowLeft;
        var as21DashboardScrollArrowRight;
        var as21DashboardDashboard;

        function scrollHandler() {
            as21DashboardScrollPos = $(this).scrollLeft()
            if (as21DashboardScrollPos > 0)
                as21DashboardScrollArrowLeft.show().css('display', 'flex');
            else
                as21DashboardScrollArrowLeft.hide();
        }

        function arrowLeftHandler() {
            const leftPos = as21DashboardDashboard.scrollLeft();
            as21DashboardDashboard.animate({scrollLeft: leftPos - 200}, 100);
        }

        function arrowRightHandler() {
            const leftPos = as21DashboardDashboard.scrollLeft();
            as21DashboardDashboard.animate({scrollLeft: leftPos + 200}, 100);
        }

        function as21DashboardShowOrHideArrows() {
            // Check if it has scroll bar
            const hasScroll = as21DashboardDashboard[0].scrollWidth > as21DashboardDashboard[0].clientWidth;
            hasScroll ? as21DashboardScrollContainer.show() : as21DashboardScrollContainer.hide();
        }

    </script>
    <script type="text/javascript">
        function refreshdashboard() {
            // ########## Variables initialization ###########
            as21DashboardScrollContainer = $(".as21-dashboard-scroll-arrow-container");
            as21DashboardScrollArrowLeft = $(".as21-dashboard-scroll-arrow-left");
            as21DashboardScrollArrowRight = $(".as21-dashboard-scroll-arrow-right");
            as21DashboardDashboard = $(".as21-dashboard-body");

            // ######### Event listeners ##########
            as21DashboardDashboard.on("scroll", scrollHandler);

            as21DashboardScrollArrowLeft.on("click", arrowLeftHandler);

            as21DashboardScrollArrowRight.on("click", arrowRightHandler);

            // Maintain scroll position among refresh
            if (typeof as21DashboardScrollPos !== 'undefined')
                as21DashboardDashboard.animate({scrollLeft: as21DashboardScrollPos}, 0);

            $(window).resize(function () {
                as21DashboardShowOrHideArrows();
            });

            // ############# Main ###################
            $(document).ready(function () {
                as21DashboardShowOrHideArrows();
            });
        }
        kwait.push(["jquery_js", function(){
            refreshdashboard();
        }]);

    </script>
    <script type="text/javascript">

	kwait.push(["jquery_js", function(){
        if (typeof 60 != 'undefined') {

            var timeInterval = 60 * 1000;

            if ($("#as21-dashboard-wrapper")) {
                setInterval(function () {
                	  if (document.hidden) return;  // Avoid refresh if page is not visible

                    $.ajax({
                        cache: true,  // Do not use cache (I don't know why)
                        url: "https://www.lastampa.it/sport/dirette/calcio/widget/dashboard/serie-a/",
                        success: function (data) {
                            const parser = new DOMParser();
                            const newDom = parser.parseFromString(data, "text/html");
                            const newElement = $(newDom).find("#as21-dashboard-wrapper").prop("outerHTML");
                            $("#as21-dashboard-wrapper").replaceWith(newElement);
                            if (typeof  refreshdashboard =="function") {
                                refreshdashboard();
                            }
                        }
                    });
                }, timeInterval);
            }
        }
	}])

</script>

  



<!-- #end http://www.lastampastatic.it/cless/common/component/dashboard/dashboard-seriea.html -->
      
     </div>
    </div>
